Conversation History - deepseek - Row: 100 - Success: False - 20260328_061308
================================================================================

Message 1
Role: system
----------------------------------------
You are an expert cloud architect and IaC engineer.
You work in two explicit phases:
  Phase 1 - Produce a typed Infrastructure Intermediate Representation (I-IR)
             as a JSON object that captures resources, their dependencies, and
             their observable effects BEFORE writing any YAML.
  Phase 2 - Compile that I-IR into a valid AWS CloudFormation YAML template.

The I-IR schema:
{
  "resources": [
    {
      "id":      "<logical name, e.g. MyBucket>",
      "kind":    "<CloudFormation resource type, e.g. AWS::S3::Bucket>",
      "fields":  { "<prop>": "<value or ref>" },
      "effects": ["<tag>, e.g. public-read | encrypted | versioned"]
    }
  ],
  "edges": [
    { "type": "depends",  "from": "<id>", "to": "<id>" },
    { "type": "connects", "from": "<id>", "to": "<id>",
      "proto": "<tcp|udp|https>", "port": <number> }
  ],
  "invariants": ["<free-text constraint, e.g. encryption-at-rest required>"]
}

Wrap the I-IR in <i_ir>...</i_ir> tags.
Wrap the final CloudFormation template in <iac_template>...</iac_template> tags.
Do NOT include raw markdown code fences inside those tags.

================================================================================

Message 2
Role: user
----------------------------------------
Analyse the following infrastructure requirement and produce
ONLY the I-IR JSON (Phase 1). Do not generate YAML yet.

Requirement:
We need a CloudFormation template that creates a standardized IAM baseline with secure, role-based access controls and cross-account trust configurations for AWS account governance. The template should:

Define IAM groups and roles (e.g., PrivilegedAdmin, RestrictedAdmin, IdentityAdmin) with granular permissions, enforcing MFA requirements for elevated actions and role assumption to enhance security.

Establish cross-account trust relationships for centralized management, allowing trusted accounts (e.g., Identity Management Account, Tooling Management Account) to assume roles while restricting sensitive operations (e.g., billing, CloudHSM) via explicit deny policies.

Provision CloudFormation and StackSet execution roles with controlled permissions for infrastructure-as-code workflows, including template validation and stack management.

Output the I-IR inside <i_ir>...</i_ir> tags.

================================================================================
